--- rcmp_custom ---
field_extra_js: class NewsEventManager {
constructor(settings) {
const { collectionTableId, jsonData, jsonExportData } = settings.poweb;
this.tableId = `#${collectionTableId}`;
this.jsonData = jsonData;
this.jsonExportData = settings.poweb.all_news.rest_export_all_news;
this.n = null;
}

formatDate(dateString) {
const dateObj = new Date(dateString);
return dateObj.toLocaleString("en-CA", {
month: "long",
day: "numeric",
year: "numeric",
});
}

upperFirst(str) {
return str ? str.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + str.slice(1) : "";
}

findColumnIndex(columnName) {
let index = -1;
const target = columnName.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "");
this.n.columns().every(function (i) {
const header = $(this.header())
.text()
.toLowerCase()
.replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "");
if (header.includes(target)) {
index = i;
return false; // stop iterating
}
return true;
});
return index;
}

processDataForTable(data) {
return data.map((item) => ({
title: `<a href=${item.view_node} class="h4">${this.upperFirst(item.title)}</a>`,
date: item.field_publish_date,
detachment: item.field_division_or_detachment,
type: this.upperFirst(item.field_news_type || item.field_event_category),
location: `<b>${item.field_location || item.field_in_person_location}, ${item.field_province_or_territory}</b>`,
province: item.field_province_or_territory,
description: `<p>${item.field_body_summary}</p>`,
}));
}

setupDataTable() {
this.n = $(this.tableId).DataTable();

const rawData = this.jsonExportData
? JSON.parse(this.jsonExportData)
: JSON.parse(this.jsonData);

const processedData = this.processDataForTable(rawData);

this.n.clear();
this.n.rows.add(processedData).draw();

this.setupFilters();
this.applyInitialFilters();
}

setupFilters() {
const minDateInput = $("#dt_mindate");
const maxDateInput = $("#dt_maxdate");
const searchInput = $('.dataTables_filter input[type="search"]');

const otherFilters = ["dt-type", "dt-province-or-territory", "dt-division-or-federal-policing-region"];
const dateColumnIndex = this.findColumnIndex("date");

$.fn.dataTable.ext.search.push((settings, data) => {
const minDate = minDateInput.val() ? new Date(minDateInput.val()) : null;
const maxDate = maxDateInput.val() ? new Date(maxDateInput.val()) : null;
const date = new Date(data[dateColumnIndex]);

const otherFiltersResult = otherFilters.every((id) => {
const filterValue = $(`#${id}`).val();
const columnIndex = $(`#${id}`).data("column");
const cellData = data[columnIndex];
return !filterValue || cellData.toLowerCase().includes(filterValue.toLowerCase());
});

if ((minDate && date < minDate) || (maxDate && date > maxDate)) return false;
return otherFiltersResult;
});

$('.wb-tables-filter .btn-default[type="reset"]').on("click", (e) => {
e.preventDefault();
$(e.target).closest("form")[0].reset();
this.clearURLQueryParams();
this.n.search("").columns().search("").draw();
});

$('.wb-tables-filter .btn[type="submit"]').on("click", (e) => {
e.preventDefault();
this.updateURLQueryParams();
this.updateDateFilters(minDateInput, maxDateInput);
this.n.draw();
});

searchInput.on("keyup", (e) => {
this.n.search(e.target.value).draw();
});
}

applyInitialFilters() {
const detachment = this.getURLQueryParameter("l");
if (detachment) {
$("#dt-division-or-federal-policing-region").val(detachment);
this.applyFilter("division-or-federal-policing-region", detachment);
}
}

applyFilter(columnName, value) {
const columnIndex = this.findColumnIndex(columnName);
if (columnIndex !== -1) {
$(`#dt-${columnName}`).val(value);
this.n.column(columnIndex).search(value).draw();
}
}

getURLQueryParameter(name) {
return new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get(name);
}

setURLQueryParameter(name, value) {
const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

if (value) {
urlParams.set(name, value);
} else {
urlParams.delete(name);
}

const path = window.location.href.split('?')[0];
const newURL = `${path}${urlParams.toString() ? `?${urlParams.toString()}` : ''}`;
history.pushState({}, '', newURL);
}

clearURLQueryParams() {
this.setURLQueryParameter("l", "");
}

updateURLQueryParams() {
this.setURLQueryParameter("l", $("#dt-division-or-federal-policing-region").val());
}

updateDateFilters(minDateInput, maxDateInput) {
const minDate = minDateInput.val();
const maxDate = maxDateInput.val();

if (minDate && !maxDate) {
maxDateInput.val(new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0]);
}

if (maxDate && !minDate) {
const maxDateObj = new Date(maxDate);
const startDate = new Date(maxDateObj.setDate(maxDateObj.getDate() - 7));
minDateInput.val(startDate.toISOString().split("T")[0]);
}
}

init() {
$(document).on("wb-ready.wb-tables", this.tableId, () => {
this.setupDataTable();
});
}
}

new NewsEventManager(drupalSettings).init();
